For example, if you're working in a cell, pressing F6 will move the focus to the ribbon, and pressing it again will cycle through other areas like task panes or the formula bar.</span></span></div></div></div><div id="m0dcZZf2I7ShseMPhZ-p4Ac__13"><div class="g"><div data-hveid="CAwQAA" data-ved="2ahUKEwjXr5edtdSCAxW0UGwGHYVPCnwQFSgAegQIDBAA"><div class="tF2Cxc"><div
